	desc = gft_tech_trade_ai.3.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = gft_tech_trade_ai.1001.c
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = gft_technology_trade_ai_tech_subspace_drive_global_flag
		}
		allow = {
			NOT = {
				has_technology = tech_subspace_drive
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
				}
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = influence
					value >= 50
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			add_resource = {
				influence = -50
			}
		}
		give_technology = {
			tech = tech_subspace_drive
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_global_flag = gft_technology_trade_ai_tech_subspace_drive_global_flag
			add_trust = {
				who = event_target:gft_tech_trade_ai_0
				amount = 50
			}
		}
	}
